      <h3>Capital Resource Management</h3> 
      <p>Capital Resource Management is responsible for development of the Capital Improvement Program, physical planning for the campus, and campus-wide space management and inventory.</p> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents.html">Available Documents</a></li> 
       <li>Capital Programs</li> 
       <li><a href="/open_pos.html">Open Positions in Capital Planning</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3>Campus Space Data</h3>

       <li><a href="/space_app.html">Space Assignment Policies and Procedures</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/space_reports.html">Campus Space Reports</a></li> 
       <li><a href="http://fms.ucr.edu/" target="blank">Facilities Management System (FMS)</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/fms_training.html">FMS Training Dates</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/files/Room%20Numbering%20Standards%20Final%2010-06.pdf" target="_blank">Room Numbering Standards document</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/CAD_Standards.pdf">CAD Standards document</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/gis_training.html">Campus GIS</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/gis_data.html">GIS Data Standards Documentation</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4><a href="/files/budget_for_capital_improvements_2003-2004.pdf" target="_blank">Riverside Campus Budget for Capital Improvements (2003-2008)</a></h4> 
      <h3>Other Links:</h3>

              <div id="watch-description-content"> 
               <div id="watch-description-clip"> 
                <p id="watch-uploader-info"> <strong>Published on <span id="eow-date" class="watch-video-date">Mar 5, 2014</span> </strong> </p> 
                <div id="watch-description-text"> 
                 <p id="eow-description">The collaboration between UC Riverside and the Sherman Indian High School has led to a more complete study of Native culture. To read UCR alumnus and University of Illinois Professor Matthew Sakiestewa Gilbert's first-person account of his research at Sherman, go to <a href="http://magazine.ucr.edu/746" target="_blank" title="http://magazine.ucr.edu/746" rel="nofollow" dir="ltr" class="yt-uix-redirect-link">http://magazine.ucr.edu/746</a>.</p>

      <h3>Reporting trouble with PPS, SIS+ or the IBM mainframe</h3> 
      <h4>Software</h4> 
      <p>Any problem reported should be supported with a listing and output, or in the case of an online system problem a list of exactly the steps you were doing leading up to the problem.</p> 
      <p>Suspected software problems should be brought to the attention of the programmer in charge of the application.</p> 
      <ul> 
       <li>Student Information System problems -- Mary Livaudais, x22072.</li> 
       <li> Payroll Personnel System problems -- Ron Ortega, x23172.</li> 
       <li>Storehouse problems -- Rich Haussner, x25132 </li> 
       <li>Equipment Management problems&nbsp; -- Richard Haussner, x25132 </li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4>Hardware</h4> 
      <p>Hardware problems are defined as terminal connection problems and printer problems related to getting data from the IBM host system. (PC problems and printer problems relating to non IBM host systems should be reported to the <a href="mailto:helpdesk@ucr.edu">Help Desk</a>, x23555).</p> 
      <ul> 
       <li>Hardware problems -- Operations personnel, x25938.</li> 
      </ul>
